View the path in real time on the installed Microsoft Here map, log your trip and save it to a GPX file.  Saved files can also be imported into Google Earth, Microsoft MapPoint or Streets and Trips and many other apps that read GPX files.\r\n\r\nDownload the app on your Windows 10 PC/tablet AND your phone.  The app and GPX files are compatible.\r\n\r\nImport/export placemarks to a local file or cloud storage file.  The files are saved in clear text XML format.  Edit them and resave in any text editor.\r\n\r\n*Important: when running the GPS, if you need to log the data be sure to start saving the data right away, that way if the app or phone/tablet happens to crash you will still have almost all the data minus a minute or two.\r\n\r\nSaved GPX files can also be used with FreeLogBook.biz to help keep electronic logbook and track mobiles within a company.  http://www.freelogbook.biz/home/\r\n\r\nNow works under lock screen or in the background!\r\n\r\nThis app is designed to be used with the GPS/GNSS Geolocation device built into some newer tablets and Windows phones.  If you don't have a GPS chip in your device then you can only view maps, you can't track your position.  (Please don't give it a 1 star rating because of something limited by your hardware and nothing to do with the app :)\r\n\r\n(The tracking does not work with an external GPS connected by USB or com port.  Even if the device is installed inside the laptop, if it is on a com port it does not work.  This is a Windows 10 thing, not the apps fault, sorry.)\r\n\r\nUpdate May 2017: I have received an unconfirmed report that it may work on a Surface Pro 4 with external USB GPS.  If you know this to be true, please contact me and tell me how you did it.\r\n\r\nThere are two different versions available depending on your operating system.  Windows 10 and Windows 8.1\r\n\r\nMain features.\r\n- Live mapping of GPS coordinates.\r\n- Load previous GPX files and replay them on the map in real time or accelerated speed.\r\n- Add 3 custom placemarks.\r\n\r\nIf your GNSS device in your tablet or phone still works outside WiFi or cellular service the logging and mapping will continue.  Windows 10, click the 'Download Maps' button to download the maps locally for your region for full offline use.\r\n\r\nThe app should also be able to load and display GPX files from other GPS devices, such as Garmin Nuvi etc.   If it does not please let me know and I might  be able to update the app so it does.
